by micromedia  @# / /
rigs brgya'i gtso bo khyab bdag rdo rje sems pa'i ngo bo skyabs rje yongs 'dzin khri byang rdo rje 'chang chen po'i mdzad rnam rin po che'i kha skong dad gsum chu gter 'phel byed zla ba'i phreng mdzes zhes bya ba bzhugs so / /
@## / /
oM swa sti /
'gyur med bde chen dbyings kyi gar / /
sgyu mar 'char ba'i sprin gyi bcud / /
phan bde'i gru char 'jo ba'i dbang / /
mchog gi dang po snying la rol / /
phul byung blo rig kun bzang rgyal ba'i ye shes khams dang ro gcig nyid du mnyam par brdal / /
sna tshogs 'phro 'du'i bstan yod sgyu ma'i stangs stabs 'dzin pas skye rgu'i yid kyi dga' ston spel / /
zab dang rgya che'i gsung gi rol mtsho tshangs chen ral pa'i rtser yang snyems pa'i dbal gyis mtho / /
dad pas bsnyen pa'i snying gi snying por gtan bde'i rlabs kyis grub gnyis 'ching ba'i mgon des skyongs / /
gang gi mdzed 'phrin kun gsal 'dzum pa'i sgo / /
gzhal 'dod byis blo'i 'dab chags gshog rtsal mthu /
@## / /
zla ba'i ma ma song ba'i rjes shul du / /
phra rdul dag byed zhugs pa 'dir mtshon bya / /
de la 'dir bdag sogs lha dang bcas pa'i skye rgu ma lus pa'i rnam par 'dren pa chen po /
gsang gsum bag yod kyi gzhi la gzhol bas nyes ltung gi rnyog pa ring du bsal te rnam par dag pa'i tshul khrims kyi bdud rtsis thugs rgyud yongs su gtams pa'i mkhan chen 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po /
bdag pas gzhan gces pa'i byang chub kyi sems rin po che'i go cha btsan po bgos te bya dka' ba'i spyod pa mtha' dag la zhum pa med par slob pa'i thugs bskyed dus su smin pa las /
'jam mgon chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha pa chen po'i lung rtogs chos kyi srid la dbang bsgyur ba'i chos kyi 'khor bsgyur chen po /
nges gsang rdo rje theg pa'i rnal 'byor la sgrub pa snying por gzhol bas zung 'jug nges don gyi dkyil 'khor bye ba rgya mtsho spro ba dang bsdu ba'i rigs kun gyi bdag po drung pa rdo rje 'chang /
gling 'dir mkhas grub yongs kyis ral pa'i zur phud gang gi zhabs mthil nor bu'i me long du mngon par gsal zhing /
snyan pa'i ba dan srid zhi'i bla na g.yo ba /
khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa'i ngo bo he ru ka pa skyabs mgon brgyal ba'i yongs 'dzin khri byang rdo rje 'chang chen po don gyi slang du mtshan nas smos te rje btsun blo bzang ye shes bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyi rnam par thar pa thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig mchis pa ste /
nges pa'i don du na ring mo zhig nas bla med sku bzhi'i go 'phang mngon du mdzad zin pa yin pas thub pa bde bar gshegs kun dang mnyam pa nyid gsum gyis mnyam zhing /
mgon po gang 'di'i mdzad pa mtha' dag kyang phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba kun dang mdzad pa mnyam par brdal ba yin te /
ji skad du /
theg pa chen po mdo sde rgyan las /
ji ltar nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyi / /
'od zer dpag tu med 'dres shing / /
rtag tu bya ba gcig la 'jug /
'jig rten la yang snang ba byed / /
de bzhin zag med dbyings na yang @# / /
sangs rgyas dpag tu med 'dres shing / /
mdzad pa gcig ni mdzad pa la / /
ye shes snang bar mdzad par 'dod / /
ces nyi ma'i 'od zer 'dres nas 'jig rten snang bar byed pa'i dpe dang sbyar nas gsungs pa dang /
yang /
rgya mtshor song bar gyur na thams cad kyang / /
gnas rnams gcig cing chu yang che la gcig /
ces sogs kyis dper na chu klung mtha' dag rgya mtsho chen por 'dres na ro gcig tu 'gyur ba bzhin /
sangs rgyas pa na rgyud tha dad pa'i mngon rtogs dang mdzad pa rgya che chung sogs kyi rnam par gzhag pa med la /
'on kyang gdul bya rang rang gi las kyis 'brel ba'i dbang gis gang la gang 'dul gyis rnam pa sna tshogs su snang rgyu yod pa yang /
de nyid las /
zag med dbyings na sangs rgyas rnams / /
mkha' ltar lus ni med phyir dang / /
sngon gyi lus rjes 'brang ba'i phyir / /
gcig min mang po nyid ma yin / /
zhes sogs gsungs pa dang /
'di nyid kyang /
'phags pa thogs med kyis mngon pa kun btus su /
bsam gyis mi khyab pa bzhir gsungs pa'i nang nas /
mi mnyam pa nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i bsam mi khyab kyi mthar thug tu gsungs pa yin la /
de lta bu'i gsang gsum gyi yon tan rnams lta ci /
sku tshe 'di nyid kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i mdzad pa rnams kyang brjod par sla ba ma yin zhing /
des ??? du mthong so so'i skye bo las dang nyon mongs pa'i 'ching ba ma lus pa dang ldan par rnams la thun mong las kyang thun mong du snang ba'i sku tshe 'di'i mdzad 'phrin rags pa tsam zhig rjod byed yi ge'i phreng bar bkra ba la /
dgung grangs bdun cu don lngar phebs pa phyi lo chig stong dgu brgya bdun cu don lnga /
bod shing yos zla ba gnyis pa'i nang bzhugs sgar rda ram sa lar dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lus dkyil gyi dbang dang zab khrid smin stsol mdzad pa'i bar skyabs rje rdo rje 'chang rang nyid kyis mdzad rnam rin po che bka' rtsom grub cing 'phrul dbar du thon zin pa dang /
'dir de nyid kyi kha skong gi tshul du sngar gyi 'phro 'thud de 'god pa la /
shing yos zla ba gnyis pa'i mar ngo'i tshes bcur chog grwa brgyad dang lhan du bla mchod bde stong dbyer ma bde mchog dang 'brel ba'i sgo nas stong tshogs 'bul gnang mdzad /
bod zla gsum pa'i tshes gcig nas bzung bcad rgya dang 'brel sgrol dkar yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgo nas tshe sgrub mdzad /
bod zla bzhi pa'i tshes gcig nas sku gzugs la tsha ba'i bsnyun gzhi'i rkyen gyis sku'i tshigs rnams bsnyun pa dang /
de'i steng snga lo mgul gyi zur du gnyan 'bur zhig 'khrungs pa de dang phyogs 'dra zhig snyan gyi rgyab tsam du 'bur po zhig thon nas bsnyun zug kyang cung zad yod par /
ye shes khyung khra'i sngags kyi bzlas @# / /
brjod mdzad pa dang /
sman pa ye shes don ldan lags kyis brtags don bzhin gsol sman nyin bzhi'i ring bzhes pas sku'i gnyan 'bur rang zhir gyur /
tsha ba'i bsnyun mnar la 'phrul zang dang ma nu bzhi thang thengs gnyis bzhes pas sku khams dwangs bskyed bzhes /
tshes brgyad nyin ring min gong sa skyabs mgon chen po ka rdor khul du chibs bsgyur bskyang nyer gyur pa dang /
skyabs rje mchog kyang sud sir chibs bsgyur mdzad rgyu'i yig cha thob tshe 'phral phebs mdzad bzhed bcas la brten /
rnga steng pho brang du gong sa skyabs mgon chen po'i sku mdun du mjal bcar zhu gnang mdzad cing /
de nyin skyabs rje yongs 'dzin dga' khri gling rin po che yang pho brang du chibs bsgyur mdzad par /
nye sngon gong sa mchog gi sku'i tshe sgrub mdzad pa'i tshe rdzas kyang 'bul gnang dang bcas lhod mjal zhu gnang mdzad /
tshes bco lnga nyin rda sa deng mdzod khang du dpe khrid zhu mkhan gyi phyi rgyal mi rib sa mang po zhig nas rgyu sbyar gyis dpe mdzod khang gi tshoms sa chen du bla ma chod tshogs 'khor rgyas pa phul ba'i dbu bzhugs su yongs 'dzin khri chen gling rin po che dang lhan du skyabs mchog gdan zhus ltar zhabs sor 'khod cing /
tshogs 'khor 'bul skabs phyi rgyal mi rigs rnams nas bla ma mchod pa'i 'don pa dbyin yig gi deb thog nas bod skad du mnyam 'don thub pa dang /
dpe khrid dge rgan dge bshes ngag dbang dar rgyas nas rta dbyangs bskul ba ltar khong tshos kyang mnyam gyer bgyis pa sogs gra 'grigs po yod par thugs dgyes tshor chen po byung /
yongs 'dzin khri chen gling rin po che gzim shag bkra shis rab brtan du chibs bsgyur bskyangs te /
skyabs rje mchog ring min phyi rgyal du chibs bsgyur mdzad rgyur phebs skyel gyi phyag rtags kyang 'bul bzhes mdzad /
bod zla lnga pa'i tshes gcig nyin rda sa'i zlos gar tshogs pa nas a ri sogs phyi rgyal du zlos gar 'khrab ston bya mi nyi shu skor zhig bskyod nyer brten /
kho tshos phyi rgyal du 'khrab bston bya rgyu'i sde tshan rnams dgong sa chen po mchog la gzigs 'bul zhu rgyur /
skyabs rje yongs 'dzin rnam gnyis dang bka' blon rnam pa bcas gzigs mor gdan zhus ltar /
rda steng zlos gar tshogs khang du phebs nas zlos gar gyi rtsed sna khag la gzigs /
de'i skabs zhus nas spyir kho bo ltad mor do snang chung ba'i thob /
de nyin sngar shA ri'i bus /
shi lpags shi ba'i rgyus pa dang /
'chi 'gyur bzhad gang 'jo sgeg gis /
'chi ba'i skye bo 'dus pa la / /
mkhas pa su zhig bag med byed / /
ces gsungs pa de dran nas kho tshos bro 'khrab pa dang /
rnga brdung ba sogs byed par ltad mo'i snang ba cher ma byung kha ton byas nas bsdad pa yin /
zhes bka' stsal /
'di'i lo rgyus rgyas pa 'dul ba lung du bzhugs pa las shes dgos shing /
skabs don mdor bsdus @# / /
shig ni /
de yang sngar ston pa zhal bzhugs pa'i dus su na la da zhes pa'i grong du ma sha ri ka dang /
pha skar rgyal gnyis kyi bu shA ri'i bu'am nye rgyal zhes grags pa zhig byung ba des pha dang lhan cig rig byed 'don pa'i tshe /
pha skar rgyal la tshig 'di'i don ci lags zhes dris pa na /
bu kho bos 'di'i don mi shes te /
gsang tshig gi gzhi 'di dag ni sngon gyi drang srong rnams kyis bstod pa bsgrags pa tsam mo zhes zer ba la /
bu nye rgyal gyis smras pa /
yab 'di'i don med dam snyam mam /
tshig 'di'i don 'di dang 'di yin no zhes don bkral te brjod pas /
skar rgyal shin tu dga' nas rang gi slob ma bram ze'i khye'u lnga brgya klog tu bcug pa'ang bu nye rgyal la btad do / /
nye rgyal gyis klog tu 'jug pa na /
rig byed ring po rnams thung ngur bzhag /
thung du rnams ring por bzhag /
tshig dang yi ge phra bar byas nas bslab bo / /
yang de'i tshe /
grong shing thags can du bram ze mdun gru 'dzin zhes pa shin tu nor mang ba'i phyug po zhig yod par /
bu pang nas skyes zhes pa'am /
rigs kyi ming mau gal gyi bu zhes pa zhig byung ba des kyang pha dang lhan cig rig byed 'don pa na /
pha gru 'dzin la 'di'i don ci lags zhes dris pa sogs sngar dang 'dra bar /
pha gru 'dzin gyis kyang khye'u lnga brgya de la btad /
de ltar phyogs gnyis ka'i khye'u rnams mi klog pa'i tshe grong khyer nang du song bar /
nye rgyal gyi slob ma rnams kyis gsang tshig 'don bzhin mdun nas song /
pang nas skyes kyi slob ma rnams phyi bzhin song bas /
khye'u mdun ma rnams la ci'i phyir gsang tshig gzhi nyams par klog ces dris par /
mdun gyi khye'u rnams kyis 'o na ji ltar yin zhes dris par /
phyi nas 'ong bas 'di ltar ro zhes lan btab /
mdun gyis khye'u rnams kyis khyed cag su las bklag ces dris bar /
pang nas skyes kyi slob ma rnams kyis de mi shes pa ni nyi zla mi shes pa ste pang nas skyes las bslab bo / /
khyed cag su las bklag ces zer bar /
nye rgyal gyi slob ma rnams kyis kyang de mi shes pa ni nyi zla mi shes pa ste /
nye rgyal las bklag go zhes brjod /
don de slob ma rnams kyis nye rgyal dang pang nas skyes so sor smras pas /
de dag gis kyang bklag tshul dngos pang nas skyes kyi slob mas bklag pa bzhin bklag dgos mod /
nye rgyal shes rab che bas 'di ltar byas so zhes zer /
de nas nye rgyal dang pang nas skyes gnyis phan tshun mthong 'dod nas /
nye rgyal pha'i sar song nas grong shing thags can du pang nas skyes phrad par 'phro 'dod ces gnang ba zhus par /
pas de khyod rang las shes rab che'am /
min gyi de shin tu phyug lags /
pha nye rgyal gyis /
mi gang rigs kyis rgan pa dang / /
na tshod rgan dang nor gyis rgan / /
de kun thos pas rgan pa yi / /
sgo na don kun gnyer bas sdod / /
gal te de 'dir 'ong na ldos? pas bgo bsha' bya yi der bgrod par mi bya'o / /
zhes dang /
de bzhin du pang nas skyes kyis kyang pha'i drung du song nas nye rgyal phrad par 'gro 'dod ce @# / /
gsol bas /
pha gru 'dzin gyis /
mi gang rigs kyis rgan pa dang / /
na tshod rgan dang thos pas rgan / /
de kun nor gyis rgan pa yi / /
sgo na ci bya snyam pas sdod / /
de 'dir 'ong na nor gyi bgo bsha' bya yi /
bgrod par mi bya'o zhes zer ro / /
de nas dus shig na rgyal po'i khab na klu'i rgyal po ri bo dang yid 'ong gnyis kyi dus ston la babs par /
rgyal po gzugs can snying po bya ba gzhan zhig byung nas bu ma skyes dgra dus ston der btang rgyu gtan 'khel /
mdun na 'don gru 'dzin gyis kyang bdag shin pang nas skyes mdun na 'don du 'gyur ro snyam nas bu pang nas skyes dus ston la btang ste /
dus ston der rgyal po dang /
mdun na 'don dang /
rgol ba dang /
mchog thob pa'i stan bzhi yod par /
rgyal po'i stan gcig pu gong du zhog la de'i 'og der 'dug cig ces dang /
skar rgyal gyis kyang de thos nas nye rgyal btang ste mchog thob pa'i stan la dbyig gu dang ril ba zhog la /
rgol ba'i stan la 'dug cig ces bsgos te btang ngo / /
de gnyis kyang dus ston der song nas de ltar 'dug pa dang /
gar mkhan rnams kyis pi wang sogs brdung nas glu blangs par brtsams pa dang /
khye'u de gnyis dbang po phyir bslan nas 'dug pa skye bo ltad mo ba phal mo ches mthong nas de dag gis 'di gnyis yang na blun po zhig go /
yang na ni shes pa mi 'khrugs pa zhig go zhes smras so / /

gang gis mthong ba dang /

pang nas skyes kyis /

glu rnams thams cad bkyal pa ste / /
gzugs kun mi rtag nyid yin no / /
zhes smras pas /

lhan cig gnas pa mchog lags kyi / /
'jig rten pha rol 'jig byed pa'i / /
mkhas pas rgyal srid slad du ni / /
gsod dang 'ching dang rdeg pa dag /
bgyid pa de lta ma lags so / /
zhes zhus kyang pha mas 'bral ba mi bzod do zhes ma gnang bar /
pang nas skyes kyis pha mas mi gnang na zan mi bza'o zhes nyin drug gi bar zas bcad pas /
pha mas khyod gzhon pas sdug bsngal ba mi shes kyi tshangs spyod dka' la /
rab tu dben pa bya dka'o / /
nye du'i tshogs kyis kyang lan gsum bar bzlog kyang bzlog ma nus par /
nye du rnams kyis pang nas skyes gum pas ci bgyi /
rab byung bya na gson par 'gyur la /
gal srid rab byung la mi spro na slar pha ma'i gnas su 'ong ngo zhes zer bas /
pha ma gnyis kyis rab tu byung ba'i gnang ba ster /
de 'bras bu'i btung bas rim gyis stobs bskyed nas nye rgyal sar song ste tshur shog dang lhan cig rab tu byung ngo / /
nye rgyal gyis khyod pha mas gnang ngam zhes dris pas /
gnang ngo zhes lan btab /
'o na ngas kyang zhu'o / /
pang nas skyes kyis kho bo yun ring po de tsam 'gor na khyed ci tsam 'gor /
nye rgyal gyis kho bo da lta rang gnang ba thob par byas nas 'ong ngo zhes pha ma'i sar song nas /
bdag rab tu byung ba'i gnang ba stsol cig /
pha mas kyang rab tu byung na khyed la legs pa yin nam zhes dris par /
nye rgyal gyis de ltar lags so / /
'o na song la rab tu byung zhig ces sngon gyi las smon gyi dbang gis 'phral du gnang ba thob ste /
rim gyis ston pa bcom ldan 'das dang mjal nas 'khor rig byed slob pa stong dang bcas tshur shog gi sgo nas bsnyen par rdzogs te mchog zung gcig tu gyur pa yin no / /
gong gi tshigs bcad shi lpags shi ba'i rgyus pa dang / /
zhes sogs kyi don ni /
glu mkhan rnams kyis rnga che chung rnams la srog chags shi ba'i pags pas g.yogs pa dang /
pi wang sogs la srog chags shi ba'i rgyus pas rgyud 'dren pa dang /
gar 'khrab mkhan rnams kyang gdon mi za bar 'chi bar 'gyur ba zhig gis 'chi ba ma dran par bzhad gad dang /
'jo sgeg gi rnam pa bstan pa la /
ltad mo ba nges bar 'chi bar 'byung ba 'ba' zhig mang du 'dus nas blta ba 'di dag la /
skye sa mtha' 'chi bar shes pa'i mkhas pa su zhig gis dga' snang dang bcas bag med la 'jug pa ji ltar rigs mi rigs so zhes pa'i don no / /
di nas sud sir chibs bsgyur mdzad rgyu gtan 'khel gyis ser skya drag zhan ches mang ba mgon po gang gi zhal dkyil mjal bar lhags pa rnams kyi re ba yongs su bkang bar mdzad /
bod tshes drug nyin gong sa skyabs mgon chen po mchog kyang glo bur gzim shag bkra shis rab brtan du zhabs 'khod kyis /
nye lam ka rdor khul du chibs bsgyur gnang skabs kyi chos srid mdzad sgo'i skor dang /
ring min dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi @# / /
ljags bsnyen bskyang bzhed sogs gsung gleng gnang ste chu tshod gnyis tsam ring lhod bzhugs mdzad /
tshes bdun nyin rda sa nas phebs thon gyis spa than ko khra nas ri li brgyud ldi lir zhabs 'khod kyis sog bla gu ru de ba'i shag tu sku ngal gsos te /
de'i phyi dro ldi li nas rgya gar gyi gnam gru chung ba zhig brgyud 'bom sbe'i bar dang /
de nas rgya gar gyi gnam gru che ba zhig tu zhugs te le b+han nor gyi rgyal sa b+hi ru kri gnam thang du babs te /
cung zad tsam sku ngal gsos rjes /
de nas thon i kra li'i rgyal sa rom gyi gnam thang du babs shing /
de nas sud si'i gnam grur zhugs te sud si'i zhing chen dzus rig tu 'byor /
der sku ngo pha lha ba mchog dang /
bod gzhung don gcod gnas nang blo chos lags /
ri kon dgon pa'i dge 'dun pa rnams dang /
brag sras sprul sku /
sad srung sprul sku /
rdza rong yab tshang dang sprul sku /
tre hor blo bzang nyi ma sogs phebs bsur bcar /
de nas phebs kror brgyud hor gen du zhabs sor 'khod /
tshes bcu nyin sku ngo pha lha ba dang /
ri kon dgon pa'i bla ma dge 'dun rnam pa /
rgyal mtshan rnam grol sogs mjal khar bcar /
phyi dro brag sras sprul sku dang /
sad srung sbrul sku sogs dang mnyam du bla mchod tshogs 'khor mdzad /
wa la 'gyi? sman khang du blo bzang nyi ma rogs su sbran nas sku ngo dpal ldan lags dang nor bu chos 'phel gnyis kyi gzugs khams la brtag dpyad byed du gtong gnang mdzad par /
sman pas khong gnyis kar gcong nad sogs med par gzugs khams gang legs 'dug ces zhus par snang /
tshes bco lnga'i nyin brag sras sprul sku dang /
blo bzang nyi ma gnyis kas rogs zhus te wa la gyi sman khang du skyabs rje rin po che'i sku khams la brtag dpyad gnang bar /
sman pa che shos hab li sgar zhes pas glog dpar 'dra min drug tsam brgyabs te brtag dpyad zhib nan zhus par /
de sngon sman khang du phebs dus las /
da res sku gzugs la gcong nad sogs med par sku khams legs pa 'dug ces zhus /
phebs lam du sku tsha bkra shis sgrol ma'i khyim du lhod bzhugs mdzad /

der brag ra skyes zhes brag ra'i gdong dang 'dra ba yod pa sogs gzigs shing /
skabs shig tu btsan yul zangs thang dmar po zhes sa gzhi ri brag thams cad dmar ba khrag gi chu rgyun 'bab pa /
khang pa dmar po thog brtsegs can /
yur ba tshun chad nas khrag gi rgyun 'bab pa /
bar bar du khrag gi ltengs ka 'khyil ba sogs yod pa gzim ltas su byung ba dang /
rmar khams dpa' bo khro 'bar gyi sring mo rta spyang mas bsti stangs bya ba'i tshul dang /
'bras spungs sgo khra lha mo khang nyams gso mdzad nyer dpal ldan lha mo dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur dang /
mgon po zhal gyi bsnyen mtshams mdzad skabs mgon pos gus btud mdzad pa'i mtshan ma ji byung mdzad rnam nyid las gsal ba ltar dang /
gzhan yang gangs dkar bla ma rin po ches rje nyid la ma mo'i bla rdo 'bul bar mdzad de 'di nyid bsten na phan grogs 'gran zla bral ba yod tshul zhus 'dug pa ltar /
bla rdo de nyid de sngon lha sar gsol lcog tu yod pa gus par mig ston mdzad pa dang sbrags gangs dkar bla ma rin po ches de bltar gsung tshul bcas bka' stsal byung ba /
rdo sgong gzugs sgong che tshad tsam zhig la dbus su mig lta bu shin tu gsal ba'i rang byon yod pa ngo mtshar che ba zhig 'dug pa sogs /
mdor na mthu ldan bstan srung dam can rgya mtshos rnam bzhi'i 'phrin las dus las skad cig kyang mi yong bar bsgrubs pa la brten nas mi mthun pa'i phyogs mtha' dag las yongs su rgyal te /
'phrin las nyin byed kyi snang ba 'dzam gling gi tha gru kun tu khyab par gyur cing /

zhes gsungs pa ltar /
'bras bu de dang de 'grub pa la med mi rung gi rgyu gang dang gang gtso che ba de nyid nan tan du bsgrubs te /
them skas kyi rim pa ltar lam 'og ma 'og ma brtan par byas pa'i mthus 'bras bu grub pa'i tshe yang /
rang dang gzhan gyi don phun sum tshogs pa mtha' dag 'grub pa yin te /
de sngon skun gzhon zhing gdan sar tshogs chos 'grims pa'i skabs dga' ldan phar khang tshan du mkhas grub rje'i phyag bzo yin par grags pa'i dpal ldan lha mo'i sku mtho gang lhag tsam zhig yod pa 'di'i phyag mdzub chag skyon song ba /
'ga' zhig gis bzo bcos kyis sbyar rung yang yang skyon shor gyis gtan nas ma 'byar ba ma zad /
khang tshan yang nang mi mthun pa dang 'dod yon nyams gud du gyur te /
rjes su skyabs rje mchog gdan zhu bgyis par skyabs rje mchog nas lho pa dge bshes byams pa bstan 'dzin zhes lha bzo ba zhig yod pa de 'khrid nas snga dro ar chog dang bzo bo lhar bskyed sogs mdzad cing /
bzo bskrun zin rjes rab gnas gnang bar brten de rjes phyag la gog skyon ma byung zhing /
phar khang tshan yang de nas bzung thugs mthun khrims gtsang dang /
'brog sde'i dkar chu 'phel rgyas shin tu che ba sogs lam 'gro je cher song ba'i stabs kyis skyabs rje mchog la dad gus chen pos yang yang gdan zhus kyis thugs 'dris che ba byung ba dang /
rjes sor khams nas yar phebs grub nas kyang pha ra khang tshan gyis sbyin bdag zhus te byang rtse grwa tshang gi 'du khang du dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang chen zhus pa sogs dad dam bla na med par gyur /
yang sku gzhon nu'i dus su mtshan zhabs pa ngag dbang blo bzang gi shag rogs dge bshes don grub ces pa nad mnar yun ring tshabs che byung bar /
skyabs mchog nas sku rtsed dang 'brel ba lta bus nad bdag stobs 'joms cho ga mdzad pas /
skyabs mchog nyid dang nad pa gnyis ka'i ltas su bud med rgan mo zhig slel por za chas bsdu 'jug gis 'gro grabs bgyings pa'i mtshan ma byung zhing /
de nas nad pa seng drag gis dus phyis rgya nag tu phebs pa'i yar lam khams brgyud phebs skabs kyang bde gnas yod pa lta bus mtshon nor longs spyod kyis dbul ba rnams la thabs lam nye tshe ba ston pas 'phral gyi gegs 'tshu bzhi zhing tshe bsod stobs 'byor rgyas pa dang /
dga' shar rdo khang yang steng dge bshes blo bzang don ldan zhes pa drang tshugs che zhing gyod dang kha mchu 'dum bsgrigs sogs kyis mtshon mi drag khug la zhu bskul bya dgos gang cir sus? kyang blo rtsal dang gtam bshad la zla med pa khang tshan rgan gras kyi @# / /
gtso bor gyur pa des kyang /
de sngon drang po'i gtam gyis rogs phan zhus pa tsam las med rung skabs shig skyabs mchog rdo khang khang tshan gyi g.yang sgrub la gdan zhus kyi g.yang gral du rgan blo don yod par /
rdzas brgyad kyi bshad pa'i gdangs dbyangs sku gong ma khri chen tshul khrims dpal ldan gyi gsung dang dbyer med du go nas g.yang gral de gar dad pas mchi ma 'byin pa dang /
de nas bzung skyabs rje mchog la kha zhe gnyis med kyi dad pa dang rogs phan zhus shing /
'das grongs skabs kyang skyabs mchog gdan zhu'i kha chems bzhag 'dug pa ltar zhabs 'khod bskyangs pa dang /
de mtshungs skyabs mchog gangs dkar gling du bzhugs skabs /
'dabs pa'i mi drag e shod yon tan zhes pa de phyogs yong zhor du mjal kha zhig tu bcar bar /

de gar 'dabs yang steng dgon du zhabs sor bkod de ser skya mi dmangs la chos 'brel yong ba'i snyan bskul zhus pa ltar /
rjes brtses bskyangs te de'i phyi lo 'dabs pa'i khul du chibs bsgyur mdzad pa sogs skye bo khengs dregs can du ma zhal mjal ba dang gsung thos pa tsam gyis dbang du gyur pa dang /
nad gdon sogs kyis gtses pa'i nyam thag pa rnams la bsrung mdud dang bdug rdzas sogs kyis zhi bar byas pa dang /
bstan pa la log par 'khub 'ga' la thugs ma mnyes pa'i tshul tsam gyis nus pa zad pa dang /
mgon po gang nyid la log par 'khu ba'i bas ma sbyor can du ma la bzlog pa sogs kyi las sbyor gang yang ma mdzad kyang rang nyes su song ba'i lo rgyus ches mang du yod pa bcas /
de ltar mthong thos kyi skye bo tshang mas bla mar bkur? zhing zhabs kyis reg pa'i rdul yang dad pa'i rten du byed /
'byor ldan rnams nas khengs dregs dor te nyid kyi slob ma dang sbyin bdag gi tshul du padma'i mtshol bung ba 'du ba bzhin du byed pa de dag thams cad kyang /

ces rigs brgya'i g+tsho po khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa'i ngo bo skyabs rje yongs 'dzin gling? byang rdo rje 'chang chen po rje btsun blo bzang ye shes bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i mdzad rnam rin po che'i kha skong dad gsum chu gter 'phel byed zla ba'i phreng mdzes zhes bya ba 'di ni rmad byung mkhyen dpyod kyi 'od zhags ring por skyong ba khri byang bla brang phyag mdzod sku ngo dpal ldan tshe ring mchog gis mjal dar nangH mdzod dang /
